                 Annapolis health equity program pushes for vaccinations, increased education in Black, Hispanic, Latino communities
                </a>
               </h2>
              </div>
              <div class="preview-text spaced spaced-top story-preview spaced-md hddn-mble hddn-dktp hddn-tbl hddn-mble" data-pb-field="description.basic" data-pb-field-type="text" data-pb-placeholder="Write blurb here.">
               For months, Annapolis has sought to address the disproportionate impact the coronavirus has had on Black, Latino and Hispanic communities. The virus has run rampant in those groups in part because they are more likely to live in multigenerational homes, work in public-facing jobs and sometimes arent aware of city resources meant to fight the virus. Now, the city has turned its efforts to distributing vaccines in those communities.

        let oInsights = window.oVa.insights ? window.oVa.insights : {}
        let oRemoveAds = oInsights.ilv ? oInsights.ilv : ''
        if(oRemoveAds.indexOf('trb_ad_2x2/728x90/970x250/970x90_1_/') != -1 && true) {
          let label = document.getElementById('label_capgaz_hp_60')
          label && label.classList.add('hddn')
          adFlag = false
        }
      }
      if(adFlag) {
        
          //FetchBids for all ads
          if (((!DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && true) || (DeviceDetection.isDesktopSize() && true)) && (true && window.apstag) && ((true && window.headertag) || (false && window.PWT))) {
            let params = {
              id: 'capgaz_hp_60',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.baltimoresun/capgaz/hp',
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true
            }
            if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor = trb.data.page.ads.vendor || {}
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams = trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams || {}
            }
            const dimensions = !'[[[2, 2], [970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], [[2, 2], [728, 90]], [[2, 2], [320, 50]]]'.length ? null : JSON.parse('[[[2, 2], [970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], [[2, 2], [728, 90]], [[2, 2], [320, 50]]]'),
              sizemapDimensions = !'[[1280, 0], [780, 0], [0, 0]]'.length ? null : JSON.parse('[[1280, 0], [780, 0], [0, 0]]')
            if (sizemapDimensions) {
              const mapping = DFPHelpers.prepareSizeMaps(dimensions, sizemapDimensions).mapping
              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['capgaz_hp_60'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)
            } else {
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['capgaz_hp_60'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }

          
            if (trb.data.ads.optimera) {
              if (!window.oPageUnload) {
                oAv.push("trb_ad_2x2/728x90/970x250/970x90_1_/");
                oVa["trb_ad_2x2/728x90/970x250/970x90_1_/"] = ["NULL"];
              } else {
                oPageUnload('trb_ad_2x2/728x90/970x250/970x90_1_/', true);
              }
            }
          
          function loadAd() {
            dfpService.appendAd({
              id: 'capgaz_hp_60',
              optimeraId: 'trb_ad_2x2/728x90/970x250/970x90_1_/',
              adType: 'leaderboard',
              slotName: '/4011/trb.baltimoresun/capgaz/hp',
              displayMobile: true,
              displayDesktop: true,
              isOOP: false,
              is5x1: false,
              dimensionsString: '[[[2, 2], [970, 250], [970, 90], [728, 90]], [[2, 2], [728, 90]], [[2, 2], [320, 50]]]',
              sizemapString: '[[1280, 0], [780, 0], [0, 0]]',
              sizemapRefresh: 'true',
              refreshOnPhotoChange: false,
              adRefreshInterval: 0,
              includeInA9: true,
              includeInIndexExchange: true,
              loadImmediately: false
            }, false, false)
          }
          loadAd();
        
      }
    })()
       </script>

      let adFlag = true
      //Check optimera smart refresh enabled or not
      if(trb.data.ads.optimera && (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) && (true)) {
        let oInsights = window.oVa.insights ? window.oVa.insights : {}
        let oRemoveAds = oInsights.ilv ? oInsights.ilv : ''
        if(oRemoveAds.indexOf('trb_ad_300x600/300x250_4_/') != -1 && true) {
          let label = document.getElementById('label_capgaz_hp_1759')
          label && label.classList.add('hddn')
          adFlag = false
        }
      }
      if(adFlag) {
        
          //FetchBids for all ads

              id: 'capgaz_hp_1759',

              includeInIndexExchange: true
            }

              trb.data.page.ads.vendor = trb.data.page.ads.vendor || {}
              trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams = trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams || {}
            }
            const dimensions = !'[[300, 600], [300, 250]]'.length ? null : JSON.parse('[[300, 600], [300, 250]]'),
              sizemapDimensions = !''.length ? null : JSON.parse('')
            if (sizemapDimensions) {
              const mapping = DFPHelpers.prepareSizeMaps(dimensions, sizemapDimensions).mapping
              const parsedMapping = DFPHelpers.parseSizeMappings(mapping)
              if (trb.data.ads.optimeraRefresh == true) {
                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['capgaz_hp_1759'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : parsedMapping}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(parsedMapping, params)
            } else {

                trb.data.page.ads.vendor.optparams['capgaz_hp_1759'] = {'params' : params, 'mapping' : dimensions}
              }
              headerBiddingAdVendorHelpers.fetchBids(dimensions, params)
            }
          }

                oAv.push("trb_ad_300x600/300x250_4_/");

                oPageUnload('trb_ad_300x600/300x250_4_/', true);
